commit 0c888a1fd2b4f7866cc6e8f6f1b03486885ff936
Author: Daniel R. Grayson <dan@math.uiuc.edu>
Date:   Sat Feb 25 12:46:02 2017 -0500

    clean up category theory notations
    
    ... put funcomp ∘ notation in a scope "functions" so it can be obtained when conflicting with compose ∘
    ... added notation reservations to the preamble, except for a few conflicts, which are noted
    ... added a scope Cat, in addition to cat, for Precategory versus precategory notation
    ... made preferred notation "F ∙ G" for "functor_composite F G"
    ... allowed both "f · g" and "g ∘ f" for "compose f g"
    ... discovered that "[ C , D , hs ] and "[ C , D ]" can coexist, so they do
    
    The one suggestion I did not take was to relocate all the Open Scope
    commands to a position after all the Require commands, since that's hard
    to do automatically.  (They were put in place mostly automatically.)

commit d45d1923ce79782c41255d150bedc862b92f55b8
Author: Daniel R. Grayson <dan@math.uiuc.edu>
Date:   Fri Feb 24 21:32:46 2017 -0500

    change "compose" notation f;;g to f·g
    
    ... and put all the category notations into a scope called "cat"
    ... and remove the file UnicodeNotations.v
    ... and change all uses of "f;;g" to "f·g"
    
    Users who formally would just load UnicodeNotations.v should now load
    the needed files from the ones formerly loaded by UnicodeNotations,
    which were these:
    
        Require Export UniMath.Foundations.Propositions.
        Require Export UniMath.CategoryTheory.precategories.
        Require Export UniMath.CategoryTheory.functor_categories.
        Require Export UniMath.CategoryTheory.opp_precat.
    
    , and also add
    
        Local Open Scope cat.
    
    to make the notations within the scope active.
    
    To use the scope without opening it, write a term of the form '(.....)%cat'.
    
    The notation "f;;g" is still present, but is deprecated.
    
    Other category theory notations were also added to the scope "cat",
    namely these:
    
        Notation "f ;; g" := (compose f g) (at level 50, left associativity, only parsing) : cat. (* deprecated *)
        Notation "f · g" := (compose f g) (at level 50, format "f  ·  g", left associativity) : cat.
        Notation "# F" := (functor_on_morphisms F)(at level 3) : cat.
        Notation "G ∙ F" := (functor_composite _ _ _ F G) (at level 35) : cat.
        Notation "F ⟶ G" := (nat_trans F G) (at level 39) : cat.
        Notation "[ C , D , hs ]" := (functor_precategory C D hs) : cat.
        Notation "C '^op'" := (opp_precat C) (at level 3, format "C ^op") : cat.
        Notation "a --> b" := (precategory_morphisms a b)(at level 50) : cat.
        Notation "C ⟦ a , b ⟧" := (precategory_morphisms (C:=C) a b) (at level 50) : cat.

commit 0b4efab9e587eb1d1323ff4ec3dbc80247b0dd59
Author: Daniel R. Grayson <dan@math.uiuc.edu>
Date:   Wed Feb 22 23:03:15 2017 -0500

    fix the Makefile
    
    resolves #555
    
    These lines
    ```
    sub/coq/configure sub/coq/configure.ml:
            git submodule update --init sub/coq
    ```
    in our makefile cause a problem when running make in parallel, because it thinks it can run
    two copies of git at the same time to make those two files -- one of the git processes
    will fail, locked out by the other.  It also involves these lines:
    ```
    sub/coq/config/coq_config.ml: sub/coq/configure sub/coq/configure.ml
            : making $@ because of $?
            cd sub/coq && ./configure -coqide "$(COQIDE_OPTION)" -with-doc no -annotate -debug -local
    ```
    whose purpose is to run the Coq configure script again when necessary.
    
    The solution is to have just one prerequisite for sub/coq/config/coq_config.ml.  We
    take out sub/coq/configure, because it's more stable.

    add funhomotsec
    
    Definition funhomotsec {X Y:UU} {Z:Y->UU} (f : X -> Y) {g g' : ∏ y:Y, Z y}
               (h : g ~ g') : (g ∘ f) ~ (g' ∘ f) := fun (x : X) => h (f x).

    clean up, add Section and isProofIrrelevant
    
    introduce `Definition Section {X:UU} (P:X->UU) := ∏ x:X, P x.` and use
    it in a few places
    
    `homot` was generalized previously to handle sections, now generalize
    `homotcomp`, and a few others
    
    introduce `Definition isProofIrrelevant (X:UU) := ∏ x y:X, x = y.`
    
    simplify proofs of `iscontraprop1inv` and `invproofirrelevance`
    
    prove `Lemma isaprop_isProofIrrelevant X : isaprop (isProofIrrelevant X).`
    
    remove `Coercion isapropifcontr : iscontr >-> isaprop.`.  It was used
    only twice and it's an untraditional use for coercion.

commit 3c78fd84a864b585f4999de085b0173e96e64e06
Author: Daniel R. Grayson <dan@math.uiuc.edu>
Date:   Wed Feb 15 14:51:12 2017 -0500

    binary operation iteration over unordered sequences
    
    Got this (finally):
    
     Definition iterop_finseq_mon {M:abmonoid} : UnorderedSequence M -> M.
     (* iterate the monoid operation over a finite sequence of elements of M *)
    
    An unordered sequence in M is a function to it from a finite set.  The proof
    uses the generalized commutativity theorem (a finite product is independent of
    the ordering).  The proof of commutativity uses the generalized associativity
    theorem (a product of products is a product).  I almost had this proof more
    than a year ago.

    prove that sums of sets with decidable equality have decidable equality

commit 18b33c141c08425ef88c2310c3b34217f5eea332
Author: Daniel R. Grayson <dan@math.uiuc.edu>
Date:   Tue Feb 7 15:04:49 2017 -0500

    improve definition of "decidable"
    
    ... so it can be used in the definition of 'isdeceq' and can be used for
    any type, not just for propositions
    
    -Definition decidable (X : hProp) : hProp :=
    -  hProppair (X ⨿ ¬X) (isapropdec X (propproperty X)).
    +Definition decidable (X:UU) := X ⨿ ¬X.
    
    -Definition isdeceq (X:UU) : UU := ∏ (x x':X), (x=x') ⨿ (x!=x').
    +Definition isdeceq (X:UU) : UU := ∏ (x x':X), decidable (x=x').

commit 7a0a8393d6f2aaae0bd8a7046a733abc02013975
Author: Daniel R. Grayson <dan@math.uiuc.edu>
Date:   Thu Feb 2 09:09:44 2017 -0500

    generalize total2_paths2
    
        Lemma total2_paths2 {A : UU} {B : A -> UU} {a1 : A} {b1 : B a1}
              {a2 : A} {b2 : B a2} (p : a1 = a2)
              (q : transportf B p b1 = b2) : a1,,b1 = a2,,b2.
    
    turns out to be a special case of this:
    
        Lemma two_arg_paths_f {A : UU} {B : A -> UU} {C:UU} {f : ∏ a, B a -> C} {a1 : A} {b1 : B a1}
              {a2 : A} {b2 : B a2} (p : a1 = a2)
              (q : transportf B p b1 = b2) : f a1 b1 = f a2 b2.
        Proof.
          intros. induction p. induction q. reflexivity.
        Defined.
    
    , and similarly for the backwards version.  We introduce the
    generalizations and use it, where possible.

commit 17a84d0366c0539771b48de00bbb2c7a6f48f380
Author: Daniel R. Grayson <dan@math.uiuc.edu>
Date:   Sat Jan 28 19:14:18 2017 -0500

    proved flattenStep
    
    It's based on a different definition of flatten, which depends on a new
    function weqstnsum_invmap_last, which should replace the inverse in
    weqstnsum.
    
    Actually, this function intervenes:
    
      Definition flatten' {X n} {m:stn n->nat} : (Π (i:stn n), stn (m i) -> X) -> (stn (stnsum m) -> X).
    
    Compare with:
    
      Definition flatten {X : UU} : Sequence (Sequence X) -> Sequence X.
    
    These two alternative phrasings are worth replicating for generalized
    associativity and generalized commutativity, too.

Author: Daniel R. Grayson <dan@math.uiuc.edu>
Date:   Thu Jan 19 16:41:19 2017 -0500

    rename some identifiers that are needlessly plural
    
        subabmonoids -> subabmonoid
        submonoids -> submonoid
        hsubtypes -> hsubtype
        subgrs -> subgr
        subabgrs -> subabgr
        subrigs -> subrig
        subrngs -> subrng
    
    Notice that for types that are not implemented as subtypes, the identifiers are
    not plural, so there is an inconsistency.  These types include gr, monoid, rng,
    hSet, hProp, rig, setwithbinop, and subset.

commit 562c2af710a60c1a6d6c19507510c956cf355ef8
Author: Daniel R. Grayson <dan@math.uiuc.edu>
Date:   Sun Jan 15 18:24:09 2017 -0500

    Construction of functions defined at a few points on types with decidable equality
    
    This seems to be useful notation, for example, in the section on homological algebra
    when making chain complexes with specified objects in one or two locations.
    
    Lemma decfun1 {X Y:UU} (i : isdeceq X) (x1:X) (y1 y':Y) : X → Y.
    Lemma decfun2 {X Y:UU} (i : isdeceq X) (x1 x2:X) (y1 y2 y':Y) : X → Y.
    Lemma decfun3 {X Y:UU} (i : isdeceq X) (x1 x2 x3:X) (y1 y2 y3 y':Y) : X → Y.

commit 7aac82ff4377d029b2f106516fd768836d6f5849
Author: Daniel R. Grayson <dan@math.uiuc.edu>
Date:   Thu Jan 12 13:04:02 2017 -0500

    enforce linear ordering of proof files
    
    We have a linear ordering of the proof files, since the packages are listed in
    the file `Makefile` and the proof files within a package are listed in
    `.package/files`.  The linear ordering is used for making the `TAGS` file.
    
    It's a good idea for the linear ordering to be compatible with the dependency
    ordering, because then the global organization of UniMath is more
    understandable, and also a search using tags will progress through the files in
    a logical ordering (e.g., a search for a global identifier will find its
    definition first).
    
    In this commit we add some lines to `Makefile` to enforce the compatibility.
    This depends on the shell being `bash`, but for all practical purposes, `bash`
    has replaced more naive Bourne shells, so this dependency is safe.

    reorganize Foundations, part 1
    
    Here we set the stage for reorganization of Foundations as envisioned in issue
    
      Basics < Combinatorics < Algebra < NumberSystems
    
    I.e., no file should require one from a subdirectory occurring later than its
    own on this list.
    
    To accomplish this we moved the basic material about natural numbers
    not depending on Algebra into Basics and put the other material into
    a new file called NumberSystems/NaturalNumbersAlgebra.v.

commit 2d5287fcee55f6ba0a7681ffef5db214f53b82e0
Author: Daniel R. Grayson <dan@math.uiuc.edu>
Date:   Wed Jan 11 11:10:05 2017 -0500

    remove lemma apevalat
    
    In pull request #527 Vladimir introduced the function `eqtohomot` to replace
    `apevalat` partially.  In this pull request I eliminate `apevalat` in favor of
    `eqhomotop`, generalizing `eqtohomot` from functions to sections to make that
    possible.  I also moved the definition of `toforallpaths` to PartA, to point
    out that the only difference between it and `eqtohomot` is the number of
    implicit arguments.
    
    Probably we should eliminate `toforallpaths` in favor of `eqtohomot` later on.

    remove submodule lablgtk
    
    Resolves #383.
    
    It turns out that there is a homebrew "tap" called "mht208/formal"
    that contains a recipe for building "ocamlfind", which is now required
    by the makefile that builds "coq".  Here we take advantage of that to
    remove the submodule "lablgtk", saving some time.
    
    Note that "lablgtk" is used only if we build coqide.

commit 9ea44794f5bf2eff053e7a71cfcecd4e418dc43b
Author: Daniel R. Grayson <dan@math.uiuc.edu>
Date:   Wed Sep 7 13:34:12 2016 -0400

    decidable proofs
    
    When trying to prove a statement that is decidable, it is not necesary
    to think about the proof, because the proof of decidability implements
    an algorithm for deciding.  All we need to do is to figure out how to
    "run" it.  The same applies to proving the negation of such a statement.
    
    Here we offer some tactics that make the notation for doing so easy.
    
    The idea is similar to the "canonical term" notation "ct", and we put it
    in the same place in the code.
    
    We illustrate the method by cleaning up 5 proofs about rational numbers
    in RealNumbers/Prelim.v, each of which seemed ad hoc.  The new proofs
    seem more uniform and involve no thought when constructing them.

commit 65f7cf9931475a60980827f12d1653916b3d7654
Author: Daniel R. Grayson <dan@math.uiuc.edu>
Date:   Mon Sep 5 13:57:42 2016 -0400

    primitive projections: fix Archimedean.v better
    
    We install a new tactic so you can choose what to do during a proof
    based on whether primitive projections are enabled.  This is important,
    because with primitive projections enabled, the parameters to "pr1" and
    "pr2" are not present, and thus index numbers of subexpressions can
    change, as happened in this case.

commit 655fe4058af0d2c4967bdb18d4c535a7c0865788
Author: Daniel R. Grayson <dan@math.uiuc.edu>
Date:   Sat Sep 3 08:21:58 2016 -0400

    clean up in preparation for primitive projections
    
    The use of "induction" or "destruct" on an element of type "total2 P"
    without explicit names for the new variables will result in invented
    names such as t, p, t0, p0, ..., but those will change to pr1, pr2,
    ... when we switch to primitive projections.  We locate fix all such
    usage by renaming the two parts of total2.  We do something similar for
    elements of type 'coprod A B'.

commit 79ce273d8ca9ba63c13d890e0d1678f656b23f81
Author: Daniel R. Grayson <dan@math.uiuc.edu>
Date:   Wed Jun 29 18:56:04 2016 -0400

    change notation for "forall"
    
    We rename our notation for ∀ to Π.
    
    We make a global definition for ∀ that applies just to families of
    propositions and yields a proposition (hProp).
    
    We change all existing uses of "forall" and ∀ to Π.  Later on, those
    that applied to hProps could be switched back to ∀.
    
    The reason we change all uses of "forall" is that ∀ is normally read as
    "for all".
    
    Here is the definition of ∀ from Propositions.v:
    
        Lemma isaprop_forall_hProp (X:UU) (Y:X->hProp) : isaprop (Π x, Y x).
        Proof. intros. apply impred_isaprop. intro x. apply propproperty. Defined.
    
        Definition forall_hProp {X:UU} (Y:X->hProp) : hProp := hProppair (Π x, Y x) (isaprop_forall_hProp X Y).
    
        Notation "∀  x .. y , P" := (forall_hProp (fun x => .. (forall_hProp (fun y => P)) ..))
          (at level 200, x binder, y binder, right associativity) : type_scope.

commit e35bf00b184515750089204097d45f365e5364b6
Author: Daniel R. Grayson <dan@math.uiuc.edu>
Date:   Wed Mar 23 17:45:28 2016 -0400

    fix notations
    
    Resolves issue https://github.com/UniMath/UniMath/issues/322 .
    
    We changed the level of Notation "x → y" from 90 to 99 to match the core
    of Coq, and we removed the Notation "f ;; g" from the Ktheory package.
    
    I don't understand exactly what provokes this incomptability -- there
    are certainly some bugs in the way Coq takes care of such things.  In
    particular, we aren't reserving any notations yet -- it's a good
    suggestion, especially if notation reservation within a given scope
    would work.

    list packages and files in forward order, and they will appear in
    the correct order in the TAGS file.  This is important when using tags
    search and find in emacs.
    
    This resolves issue #284.
